  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b14051b0-8822-47bb-ab85-17a9eee03445'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText11209594752687208564" style="display:none">One driven woman. Five passionate paths to the perfect love.<br /><br />Chloe refuses to compromise when it comes to romance and success. Powering through her sophomore-level college business classes, she’s done with the effort of distance-dating her high-school sweetheart. But when he proposes just as she hits it off with a hunky basketball player, she worries following her heart could send her bright future to the bench.<br /><br />As Chloe matures becoming a rising star in the fashion industry, love knocks another four times. But while each potential suitor eventually pops the question, only she knows her ultimate happy ending.<br /><br />Whose arms will embrace Chloe when she chooses her forever man?<br /><br />Perfect is a standalone clean contemporary romance. If you like tender moments, lighthearted comedy, and endings you choose yourself, then you’ll adore Tricia Copeland’s option-filled tale.<br /><br />Buy Perfect to pick your ideal walk down the aisle today!</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3228028760" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14785903608308980415">This is a romance novel unlike any other; it is creative, mesmerizing, witty, and has plenty of unexpected plot twists. Tricia Copeland grabs your attention from the very first page and holds onto it until the book's last words. This is the type of story you will want to read in one go; indulge yourself and dedicate a gray and rainy Sunday to enjoying the emotional rollercoaster the lead character goes on, but be prepared to get hooked on Copeland's writing style. <br/><br/>The book is both hilarious and </span>
  <span id="freeText14785903608308980415" style="display:none">This is a romance novel unlike any other; it is creative, mesmerizing, witty, and has plenty of unexpected plot twists. Tricia Copeland grabs your attention from the very first page and holds onto it until the book's last words. This is the type of story you will want to read in one go; indulge yourself and dedicate a gray and rainy Sunday to enjoying the emotional rollercoaster the lead character goes on, but be prepared to get hooked on Copeland's writing style. <br /><br />The book is both hilarious and thought-provoking and will be a massive hit with anyone who is a fan of romantic literature. It appeals to a broad spectrum of readers, both young and old. With this book, you should expect the unexpected, with an unlikely ending that even this most inquisitive reader will struggle to predict. Do not underestimate Copeland; she is a witty and intelligent author who is a credit to the romance genre.<br /></span>

<div id="review_3190485288" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3190485288" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3190485288?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3190485288" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13204014137042890538">‘I was going to say I love you. Yes. It’s perfect’<br/><br/>Author Tricia Copeland is originally from Georgia but now lives in Denver, Colorado and pens Young Adult novels with a paranormal tilt. Her books to date include Drop of Sunshine, Lovelock Ones, and two series – the Being Me series of five books, The Kingdom Journals of four books, and now a new stand alone novel – PERFECT. <br/><br/>One of the many aspects of Tricia’s writing, be it in her highly acclaimed paranormal novels or her stand alone romance nove</span>
  <span id="freeText13204014137042890538" style="display:none">‘I was going to say I love you. Yes. It’s perfect’<br /><br />Author Tricia Copeland is originally from Georgia but now lives in Denver, Colorado and pens Young Adult novels with a paranormal tilt. Her books to date include Drop of Sunshine, Lovelock Ones, and two series – the Being Me series of five books, The Kingdom Journals of four books, and now a new stand alone novel – PERFECT. <br /><br />One of the many aspects of Tricia’s writing, be it in her highly acclaimed paranormal novels or her stand alone romance novels, is her immediate connection with the reader by her gracious use of contemporary language in a tone that feels conversational (remember when we all use to have in-person conversations rather than texting and selfies?) and comfortably invites us into her characters’ personalities. In PERFECT, she escorts us through periods of romantic incidents of a young lass longing for finding Mr. Perfect. And she doesn’t stop with ‘engagements:’ Tricia creates a character in Chloe who bonds ideals of fruitful and meaningful living with finding an accompany force to match.<br /><br />Supporting the above comment, Tricia opens her story with a longing from her character Chloe – “I miss Adam. It’s been a month since we’ve seen each other. I don’t know if I can do this anymore.” And swiftly her longed for Adam appears and proposes and a chain of events begins, one that carries through to the end. Comfortable atmosphere delivered with a wry humor – a fine opening for this interesting novel.<br /><br />The synopsis of the plot distills the story well – ‘Chloe is smart, and driven to achieve the life she's envisioned for herself, but she also longs to find that special someone to spend it with. But how do you know when your current love is the one? Chloe refuses to compromise when it comes to romance and success. Powering through her sophomore-level college business classes, she’s done with the effort of distance-dating her high-school sweetheart. But when he proposes just as she hits it off with a hunky basketball player, she worries following her heart could send her bright future to the bench. As Chloe matures becoming a rising star in the fashion industry, love knocks another four times. But while each potential suitor eventually pops the question, only she knows her ultimate happy ending. Whose arms will embrace Chloe when she chooses her forever man?’<br /><br />Tricia allows her romance to develop gradually, due in part to her accessible writing skills, but also to her colorful imagination and wry wit. With PERFECT, Tricia proves she is a first class conjurer of pure romance novels. Enhancing the pleasure of reading this book are the fine illustrations peppered throughout. Tricia continues to impress. Recommended for a wide audience. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13204014137042890538" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14681935380167161459" style="display:none">Just as the title suggests, I found the experience of reading it to be the same.<br /><br />Driven Chloe certainly knows what she wants, but will she get her happy ending? That was the premise that drew me in to read this wonderful novel by Copeland, and what a well-written story I found it to be. As I accompanied Chloe on her journey I found moments that made me smile as well as laugh. Of course it wasn’t all plain sailing, but by the end of the book I felt utterly moved and fulfilled for having read to the end. It’s something of a cliche, but Perfect was a real page turner!.All in all a great book with genuine emotion and substance. I’m sure fans of contemporary romance will live this as much as I did. </span>

  <span id="freeText9666131901027274471" style="display:none">I read an advance copy of Perfect by Tricia Copeland, which tells the story of Chloe, and how she navigates her new adult life through college and into the working world. <br /><br />Copeland does a good job of drawing the reader in, and I found myself riding along with Chloe on the emotional rollercoaster of her life, and throughly enjoying the ride! Chloe is both a relatable, and an inspiring, character. Like many young women today, she has to discover for herself what she wants out of life, how to balance the demands of college and work, while finding the "Perfect" love. While much of this book focuses on Chloe's love life, it also shows what a driven young women Chloe is, and how, even with the ups and downs of her romantic life, she is still able to work her way up the corporate ladder.</span>

  <span id="freeText5064947871234193379" style="display:none">Perfect is a fun and thought-provoking book to read because of its varying life paths structure. I’m always intrigued by the thought of how the big choices we make determine the path of our lives. Main character Chloe has to make such choices regarding college and career as well as in her love life. She has a good group of friends and a string of love interests, and her interactions with them are engaging. I especially enjoyed the author’s character development, descriptions of settings, and wit. Also, the ending was “perfect” for this story. I highly recommend this book. </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3224456636" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2233060834322634363">This is the second Copeland book I’ve read (with the first being part of her Kindgom Journals series), and though I enjoyed that book, this one was a much easier read for me (as far as flow and style). It’s like a romance mystery, and it’s not racy/lewd like we often see in romance stories. <br/><br/>This book is unique in that it’s written with reader involvement in mind. Chloe is a solid character and is clearly driven by what she wants, even if she doesn’t seem sure of it at times. The character is not</span>
  <span id="freeText2233060834322634363" style="display:none">This is the second Copeland book I’ve read (with the first being part of her Kindgom Journals series), and though I enjoyed that book, this one was a much easier read for me (as far as flow and style). It’s like a romance mystery, and it’s not racy/lewd like we often see in romance stories. <br /><br />This book is unique in that it’s written with reader involvement in mind. Chloe is a solid character and is clearly driven by what she wants, even if she doesn’t seem sure of it at times. The character is not a hyper-emotional one, but Chloe has very apparent emotional depth we can feel. The lines in the book are relatable, and a good number of Chloe’s words and feelings are easily quotable phrases that run parallels to [our] very own lives. <br /><br /> <br /><br />Copeland did a wonderful job here. She deserves all the praise and attention (and more) that this book receives. This just goes to show us that this author is versatile and creative beyond any single genre. </span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText15854609835337921419" style="display:none">4 Stars<br /><br />Perfect by Tricia Copeland is an intriguing take on contemporary romance. Ms. Copeland’s creative way of bringing this story together, and the way she involves her readers- really made for a great read. This story is a little different from the other books that I have read from Ms. Copeland- and showcases her storytelling talents and confirms that she is able to tackle any genre. <br />The premise of this book really intrigued me, and I loved the simple and elegant cover- and having enjoyed Ms. Copeland’s other work, I happily grabbed a copy to entertain me for an afternoon.<br />Perfect is a standalone, light-hearted, interesting, and thought provoking read. It has emotion, humour, sweet and tender scenes, a ‘clean’ romance, and great characters. I enjoyed the way the story was woven, even if it was a little predictable at times.<br />Looking forward to seeing what Ms. Copeland does next!<br /><br />Thank you, Tricia Copeland!<br /></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1688264818946195028">I have read novels by Tricia Copeland before and loved them but this one has to take the cake and be my top favorite of hers. I love how Copeland gave this classic of a romance read and happily ever after and turned it around to something unique and different that we never knew we were missing. I loved how this book gives us a look at the complicated life that is dating as a young woman. We see the main character Chloe working through several different relationships and the emotions and changes </span>
  <span id="freeText1688264818946195028" style="display:none">I have read novels by Tricia Copeland before and loved them but this one has to take the cake and be my top favorite of hers. I love how Copeland gave this classic of a romance read and happily ever after and turned it around to something unique and different that we never knew we were missing. I loved how this book gives us a look at the complicated life that is dating as a young woman. We see the main character Chloe working through several different relationships and the emotions and changes in her that take place. I am not going to give the rundown of the relationships because I think that is where a lot of the character development is involved in this novel. It would just ruin too much of the plot but I can tell you that this book explores all of the issues that you could think of and makes you feel a little less insecure of the history you may have. I laughed and cheered for and with Chloe and I foresee a lot of others finding that within the pages of the novel. I look forward to seeing what we will see next from Tricia Copeland.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3238597745" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5146935403772984960">[English review + Reseña en español]<br/><br/><i>Perfect</i>, by Tricia Copeland<br/>True Bird Publishing LLC. 2020<br/>280 pages.<br/>Genre / Thematic: Romance / Contemporary Romantic Comedy<br/><br/>In the search of Mr. Perfect and professional success, the intelligent and determined young Chloe Hahn Pham, about to finish her university career, shuffles her options and lives her youth while deciding unhurriedly the direction that her adult life will take. Multiple candidates appear on the sentimental horizon, and both Chloe's family a</span>
  <span id="freeText5146935403772984960" style="display:none">[English review + Reseña en español]<br /><br /><i>Perfect</i>, by Tricia Copeland<br />True Bird Publishing LLC. 2020<br />280 pages.<br />Genre / Thematic: Romance / Contemporary Romantic Comedy<br /><br />In the search of Mr. Perfect and professional success, the intelligent and determined young Chloe Hahn Pham, about to finish her university career, shuffles her options and lives her youth while deciding unhurriedly the direction that her adult life will take. Multiple candidates appear on the sentimental horizon, and both Chloe's family and friends will be there to support her when her head gets spinning around, trying to decide who will be the chosen one. At the professional level, the options are also several: from keeping the accounting of a ranch close to home to becoming a star in the fashion business. Will the perfect future be what she has imagined or will some accident of fate change the course of her life?<br /><br />Torn between Kentucky, New York and Paris, but also between school, work, family and romance, Chloe's story is, above all, a contemporary story of growth towards maturity and the search for personal success, directed by the motto "give what you have and never settle for less than you deserve".<br /><br />A simple, fun, smart and sparkling read. Recommended if you like light romance and the idea of keeping your options open.<br /><br />---------<br /><br /><i>Perfect</i>, por Tricia Copeland<br />True Bird Publishing LLC. 2020<br />280 páginas.<br />Género / Temática: Romance / Comedia Romántica Contemporánea<br /><br />En la búsqueda de Don Perfecto y del éxito profesional, la inteligente y decidida joven Chloe Hahn Pham, pronta a terminar su carrera universitaria, barajea sus opciones y vive su juventud mientras decide sin prisas el rumbo que tomará su vida adulta. Múltiples candidatos aparecen en el horizonte sentimental, y tanto la familia como las amigas de Chloe estarán ahí para apoyarla cuando su cabeza dé vueltas tratando de decidir quién será elegido. En el ámbito profesional, las opciones también son varias: desde llevar la contabilidad de un rancho cerca de casa hasta convertirse en una estrella en el negocio de la moda. ¿Será el futuro perfecto lo que ella ha imaginado o algún accidente del destino cambiará el rumbo de su vida?<br /><br />Dividida entre Kentucky, Nueva York y París, pero también entre la escuela, el trabajo, la familia y el romance, la historia de Chloe es, ante todo, una historia contemporánea de crecimiento hacia la madurez y de búsqueda de éxito personal, dirigida por la consigna de “da lo que tengas y jamás te conformes por menos de lo que mereces”.<br /><br />Una lectura sencilla, divertida, inteligente y con chispa. Recomendable si te gusta el romance ligero y la idea de mantener tus opciones abiertas.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5146935403772984960" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText12458253822313527361" style="display:none">Perfect<br />By Tricia Copeland<br />5 out of 5 stars<br /><br />I loved reading the book Perfect by Tricia Copeland. It is a romance story that pulled me in from the beginning and didn’t let me go until I read the last page. I loved reading about the character of Chloe. She is a young woman who is driven to succeed in the fashion industry. She is intelligent and independent. She also finds love and romance knocking at her door. Will she find her happy ending? I liked reading about Chloe and felt that the author does a wonderful job in developing and making her a character that I grew to care about and wanted her to be happy. The story is told from her POV. There are lighthearted moments that made me smile. This is a story about life and romance that you will not soon forget. I also enjoyed reading about the additional characters in the book that Chloe interacts with. This is a story that you will not want to put down once you have started it. I highly recommend reading it. <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText2344063259595363391" style="display:none">I have quickly come to love Tricia Copeland books. Perfect was my first romance novel by her, and it was much different. It is written in a very unique way, and it took me a while to catch on. I don't want to give anything away so I wont say much about it, but its very different from anything I've read before.<br />The story follows Chloe from college, and through the next decade or so. She is an amazing female lead, because she is independent and brilliant and successful. She knows what she wants, and isn't afraid to go after it, even if it means compromising relationships along the way. She doesn't have a type, and I actually kind of loved all the men she dated throughout the story. From her high school sweetheart to a college basketball player, fashion industry, to IT. This book gives you a happily ever after, that you didn't see coming. Or at least, I didn't see it coming! Read it, you won't regret it. <br /></span>

She was missing him immensely, however when he shows up one day surprising her and sharing some news with her, she ends up making a very hard decision. Chloe has a vision of her future and the life she wants, she is determined to get it. <br /><br />Who will she choose for her HEA?<br /><br />Moving forward Chloe has quite the journey to finding her HEA. I had some LOL moments along with some hard moments with her. This was a great story of finding the Perfect life for yourself and being happy. I really enjoyed Chloe and all of the other characters, they added a great element to the story. The author pulls you right in with her writing. 1-click and get started today.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17378572877484848094">Perfect by Tricia Copeland is a sweet romance as Chloe Hahn Pham pursues her dream in the fashion business with periodic romantic side-tracks. Each of her boyfriends possesses a unique charm and masculine quality that makes her heart flutter. Only one man is perfect for Chloe in every way. Things come to a head when an accident causes Chloe to view where she is headed with a new flame and an old flame. <br/><br/>Tricia Copeland keeps her romance novels sweet, with a plot that unfolds into a rewarding read</span>
  <span id="freeText17378572877484848094" style="display:none">Perfect by Tricia Copeland is a sweet romance as Chloe Hahn Pham pursues her dream in the fashion business with periodic romantic side-tracks. Each of her boyfriends possesses a unique charm and masculine quality that makes her heart flutter. Only one man is perfect for Chloe in every way. Things come to a head when an accident causes Chloe to view where she is headed with a new flame and an old flame. <br /><br />Tricia Copeland keeps her romance novels sweet, with a plot that unfolds into a rewarding read. Perfect depicts a modern young woman who knows her worth without a relationship defining her. Though she desires love and a companion, she isn't settling for just anyone. I found this novel refreshing with the characters well-defined and likable. Chloe knows herself and what works for her, though her mom and friends try helping her find love. This novel is humorous at times as Chloe needs a little aid from her friends. This author keeps her romances inspirational and clean, focusing on the bond that builds the relationship. <br /></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3348039907" />
    <a title="Felicia  Bates" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43542194-felicia-bates"><img alt="Felicia  Bates" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1509379926p2/43542194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3348039907?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Felicia  Bates" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Felicia  Bates" href="/user/show/43542194-felicia-bates">Felicia  Bates</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3348039907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16994144794350156071">Perfect <br/>Tricia Copeland<br/>3 out of 5 stars <br/><br/>I have read and loved books by Tricia Copeland in the past so I didn't hesitate to give Perfect a try. Overall, it was a fun, easy to read, clean romance that read very quickly. <br/>At times I felt confused about how much time had lapsed within the pages, especially within the first half of the book. I enjoyed the growth we experience with Chloe through the several years the book takes place and the progressions each of her relationships take. There were times</span>
  <span id="freeText16994144794350156071" style="display:none">Perfect <br />Tricia Copeland<br />3 out of 5 stars <br /><br />I have read and loved books by Tricia Copeland in the past so I didn't hesitate to give Perfect a try. Overall, it was a fun, easy to read, clean romance that read very quickly. <br />At times I felt confused about how much time had lapsed within the pages, especially within the first half of the book. I enjoyed the growth we experience with Chloe through the several years the book takes place and the progressions each of her relationships take. There were times I had to remember myself that Chloe's story spans several years and the decisions and experiences she has didn't happen close together. While I did enjoy Chloe as a main character, my favorite character in the book was Isaac and I loved the dynamic between him and Chloe. <br />Overall, this was an entertaining read and I would read more by Tricia Copeland in the future. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16994144794350156071" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LWyi4kZetlgDpk9dnB6cI8fXj9yUzbJ2wUGsQCqC36UfuhodiPQJIjd3li+iwlw38MdcDmdcf9lrLViIRhDvfQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
